 int main() {
 struct pollfd myfds;
 int ret;
/* check for Darwin bug with respect to "devices" */
 myfds.fd = open("/dev/null", 1); /* O_WRONLY */
 if (myfds.fd < 0)
 myfds.fd = 0;
 myfds.events = POLLIN;
 myfds.revents = 0;
ret = poll(&myfds, 1, 100);
if (ret < 0 || (myfds.revents & POLLNVAL)) {
 ret = -1;
 } else {
 int fd = 0;
 if (!isatty(fd)) {
 fd = open("/dev/tty", 2); /* O_RDWR */
 }
if (fd >= 0) {
 /* also check with standard input */
 myfds.fd = fd;
 myfds.events = POLLIN;
 myfds.revents = 0;
 ret = poll(&myfds, 1, 100);
 } else {
 ret = -1;
 }
 }
 return(ret < 0);
 }
